Dear colleagues, students, and guests of our city!
We would like to inform you that starting from today the entrance to the canteen at the 1st campus from the street will be opened from 8.00 a.m. till 8.00 p.m. for your convenience. The entrance is carried out through the access control system, via University security cards. The entrance to the canteen from the campus is also carried out through the access control system, via University security cards.
Guests without admittance cards will be able to enter the canteen from the street, security will allow them to enter.
